00010000 <_start>:
*            [&boot_info]
*    esp ->  [返回地址]
*   所以要想访问到&boot_info，则只需从当前esp的位置偏移+4字节即可
*/
_start:
    mov %esp, %ebp      //栈空间最好只用ebp来进行偏移访问
   10000:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
    mov 0x4(%ebp), %eax //将&boot_info的值存入eax中
   10002:	8b 45 04             	mov    0x4(%ebp),%eax

    push %eax           //外部函数将参数压入栈中，再进行函数调用
   10005:	50                   	push   %eax
    call kernel_init    //调用内核初始化函数
   10006:	e8 4a 18 00 00       	call   11855 <kernel_init>

    //完成内核初始化后，进行直接跳转，以替换cs寄存器中临时的内核代码段的选择子为此时内存中真正的内核代码段选择子
    //cs:KERNEL_SELECTOR_CS, ip:gdt_reload
    jmp $KERNEL_SELECTOR_CS, $gdt_reload    
   1000b:	ea 12 00 01 00 08 00 	ljmp   $0x8,$0x10012

    mov $KERNEL_SELECTOR_DS, %ax

00010298 <simple_switch>:

    .text
    .global simple_switch
simple_switch:  //simple_switch(from, to)
    //1.获取参数
    mov 8(%esp), %edx   //获取 to, 地址(指针) --> 目标任务的栈空间对应的 esp 的值
   10298:	8b 54 24 08          	mov    0x8(%esp),%edx
    mov 4(%esp), %eax   //获取 from, 地址(指针) --> 当前任务的栈空间对应的 esp 的值
   1029c:	8b 44 24 04          	mov    0x4(%esp),%eax


    //2.被调用者保存当前任务的 ebp, ebx, esi, edi 到当前任务的栈中
    //eax, ecx, edx, eip, eflags 已由调用者压入当前任务的栈中
    push %ebp
   102a0:	55                   	push   %ebp
    push %ebx
   102a1:	53                   	push   %ebx
    push %esi
   102a2:	56                   	push   %esi
    push %edi
   102a3:	57                   	push   %edi

    //3.更新当前任务栈空间的 esp
    mov %esp, (%eax)
   102a4:	89 20                	mov    %esp,(%eax)

    //3.进行栈任务栈的切换
    mov (%edx), %esp
   102a6:	8b 22                	mov    (%edx),%esp


    //4.恢复切换后的任务状态，ebp, ebx, esi, edi 手动恢复
    //eax, ecx, edx, eip, eflags, 是在当前任务(c函数)调用simple_switch时已压入当前任务栈中，
    //调用 ret 后会自行弹出并恢复
    pop %edi
   102a8:	5f                   	pop    %edi
    pop %esi
   102a9:	5e                   	pop    %esi
    pop %ebx
   102aa:	5b                   	pop    %ebx
    pop %ebp
   102ab:	5d                   	pop    %ebp

    //5.恢复切换后的任务执行流，相当于此时 esp ->[eip]， 即 pop %eip
   102ac:	c3                   	ret

000106ab <far_jump>:
 * @brief  远跳转，当跳转发生在TSS段之间时，cpu将会保存状态到当前TR寄存器指向的TSS段
 *
 * @param selector 选择子
 * @param offset 跳转的偏移量
 */
static inline void far_jump(uint32_t selector, uint32_t offset) {
   106ab:	55                   	push   %ebp
   106ac:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   106ae:	83 ec 10             	sub    $0x10,%esp
  // 传入远跳转需要的参数, 即cs = selector, eip = offset 
  uint32_t addr[] = {offset, selector};  
   106b1:	8b 45 0c             	mov    0xc(%ebp),%eax
   106b4:	89 45 f8             	mov    %eax,-0x8(%ebp)
   106b7:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   106ba:	89 45 fc             	mov    %eax,-0x4(%ebp)

  __asm__ __volatile__("ljmpl *(%[a])" : : [a] "r"(addr));
   106bd:	8d 45 f8             	lea    -0x8(%ebp),%eax
   106c0:	ff 28                	ljmp   *(%eax)
}
   106c2:	90                   	nop
   106c3:	c9                   	leave  
   106c4:	c3                   	ret    

000106c5 <write_tr>:
 * @brief   写入当前任务的TSS段描述符的选择子到TR寄存器中，告诉cpu当前段的TSS位置
 *          以便在进行任务切换时，将状态保存到该TSS段中
 * 
 * @param tss_selector 准备运行的任务的TSS段的选择子
 */
static inline void write_tr(uint16_t tss_selector) {
   106c5:	55                   	push   %ebp
   106c6:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   106c8:	83 ec 04             	sub    $0x4,%esp
   106cb:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   106ce:	66 89 45 fc          	mov    %ax,-0x4(%ebp)
  __asm__ __volatile__("ltr %[v]" : : [v]"r"(tss_selector));
   106d2:	0f b7 45 fc          	movzwl -0x4(%ebp),%eax
   106d6:	0f 00 d8             	ltr    %ax
}

//定义全局唯一的任务管理器对象
static task_manager_t task_manager;


static void switch_to_tss(uint16_t tss_selector) {
   106dc:	55                   	push   %ebp
   106dd:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp

   106e5:	66 89 45 fc          	mov    %ax,-0x4(%ebp)

    far_jump(tss_selector, 0);

 * @param limit 该段的段界限，是一个偏移量，表示段中最大的偏移界限
 * @param attr 该段的属性位
 */
void segment_desc_set(uint16_t selector,  uint32_t base, uint32_t limit, uint16_t attr) {

   10d88:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   10d8a:	83 ec 18             	sub    $0x18,%esp
   10d8d:	8b 55 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%edx

   10d97:	66 89 45 e8          	mov    %ax,-0x18(%ebp)
    //1. 获取该段描述符在内存中的起始地址，selector >> 3 取出3~15位才是其在全局描述符中的下标
    segment_desc_t *desc = gdt_table + (selector >> 3);

   10d9f:	66 c1 e8 03          	shr    $0x3,%ax
   10da3:	0f b7 c0             	movzwl %ax,%eax

   10db4:	89 c2                	mov    %eax,%edx
   10db6:	8b 45 fc             	mov    -0x4(%ebp),%eax
   10db9:	66 89 50 02          	mov    %dx,0x2(%eax)
    desc->base23_16 = (uint8_t)(base >> 16);

   10dc0:	c1 e8 10             	shr    $0x10,%eax
   10dc3:	89 c2                	mov    %eax,%edx
   10dc5:	8b 45 fc             	mov    -0x4(%ebp),%eax
   10dc8:	88 50 04             	mov    %dl,0x4(%eax)
    desc->base31_24 = (uint8_t)(base >> 24);
   10dcb:	8b 45 0c             	mov    0xc(%ebp),%eax
   10dce:	c1 e8 18             	shr    $0x18,%eax
   10dd1:	89 c2                	mov    %eax,%edx

   10dd6:	88 50 07             	mov    %dl,0x7(%eax)

    //3. 设置段界限
    if (limit > 0xfffff) { //limit大于了20位能表示的最大值

   10de0:	76 1d                	jbe    10dff <segment_desc_set+0x78>
        //将limit的粒度设置为 4kb，即将属性位G置1
        desc->attr |= 0x8000;

   10de5:	0f b7 40 05          	movzwl 0x5(%eax),%eax
   10de9:	66 0d 00 80          	or     $0x8000,%ax

        //将limit改成以 4kb 为单位
        limit /= (4 * 1024);

   10df9:	c1 e8 0c             	shr    $0xc,%eax
   10dfc:	89 45 10             	mov    %eax,0x10(%ebp)

    }
    desc->limit15_0 = (uint16_t)limit;
   10dff:	8b 45 10             	mov    0x10(%ebp),%eax
   10e02:	89 c2                	mov    %eax,%edx
   10e04:	8b 45 fc             	mov    -0x4(%ebp),%eax
   10e07:	66 89 10             	mov    %dx,(%eax)
    desc->attr |= ((uint16_t)(limit >> 8) & 0x0f00); //将limit高4位赋值到attr的8~11位(段界限的高4位)
   10e0a:	8b 45 fc             	mov    -0x4(%ebp),%eax

   10e21:	8b 45 fc             	mov    -0x4(%ebp),%eax
   10e24:	66 89 50 05          	mov    %dx,0x5(%eax)

    //4.设置属性位
